<pr_description>
Using dynamic styles with StyleX constants from defineConsts
### Describe the issue

When using a dynamic function as a style value in `stylex.create` together with a constants from a StyleX constants file (`defineConsts`), the following error occurs:

```bash
/stylex/packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/__fixtures__/main.stylex.js: Invalid pseudo or at-rule.

      68 |       )
      69 |     ) {
    > 70 |       throw new Error(messages.INVALID_PSEUDO_OR_AT_RULE);
         |             ^
      71 |     }
      72 |     if (conditions.includes(key)) {
      73 |       throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);

      at validateConditionalStyles (src/shared/preprocess-rules/basic-validation.js:70:13)
      at validateConditionalStyles (src/shared/preprocess-rules/basic-validation.js:42:9)
      at styleXCreateSet (src/shared/stylex-create.js:57:22)
      at transformStyleXCreate (src/visitors/stylex-create.js:169:19)
      at PluginPass.CallExpression (src/index.js:311:30)
      at call (../../../node_modules/@babel/traverse/src/visitors.ts:303:14)

```

### Expected behavior

Correct style transformation using constants as dynamic styles

### Steps to reproduce

Add styles as in `test case` section

### Test case

```js
// packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/transform-stylex-defineConsts-test.js

test('dynamic styles with StyleX constants', () => {
      const { code, } = transformWithInlineConsts(`
        import * as stylex from '@stylexjs/stylex';
        import { mediaQueries } from './constants.stylex';

        export const styles = stylex.create({
          nodeEnd: (animationDuration) => ({
            transition: {
              [mediaQueries.reduceMotion]: 'none',
              default: \`transform \${animationDuration}ms ease-in-out\`,
            },
          }),
        });
      `);

      expect(code).toMatchInlineSnapshot(`
        "
          // Transformation result
        "
      `);
    });
```

### Additional comments

    10	import * as messages from '../messages';
    11	import { isPlainObject } from '../utils/object-utils';
    12	
    13	export function validateNamespace(
    14	  namespace: mixed,
    15	  conditions: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
    16	): void {
    17	  if (!isPlainObject(namespace)) {
    18	    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_NAMESPACE_VALUE);
    19	  }
    20	  const ns: { +[string]: mixed } = namespace;
    21	  for (const key in ns) {
    22	    const val = ns[key];
    23	    if (val === null || typeof val === 'string' || typeof val === 'number') {
    24	      continue;
    25	    }
    26	    if (Array.isArray(val)) {
    27	      for (const v of val) {
    28	        if (v === null || typeof v === 'string' || typeof v === 'number') {
    29	          continue;
    30	        }
    31	        throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_ARRAY_VALUE);
    32	      }
    33	      continue;
    34	    }
    35	    if (isPlainObject(val)) {
    36	      if (key.startsWith('@') || key.startsWith(':')) {
    37	        if (conditions.includes(key)) {
    38	          throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);
    39	        }
    40	        validateNamespace(val, [...conditions, key]);
    41	      } else {
    42	        validateConditionalStyles(val as $FlowFixMe);
    43	      }
    44	      continue;
    45	    }
    46	
    47	    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
    48	  }
    49	}
    50	
    51	type ConditionalStyles = $ReadOnly<{
    52	  [key: string]: string | number | ConditionalStyles,
    53	}>;
    54	
    55	function validateConditionalStyles(
    56	  val: ConditionalStyles,
    57	  conditions: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
    58	): void {
    59	  for (const key in val) {
    60	    const v = val[key];
    61	    if (
    62	      !(
    63	        key.startsWith('@') ||
    64	        key.startsWith(':') ||
    65	        // This is a placeholder for `defineConsts` values that are later inlined
    66	        key.startsWith('var(--') ||
    67	        key === 'default'
    68	      )
    69	    ) {
    70	      throw new Error(messages.INVALID_PSEUDO_OR_AT_RULE);
    71	    }
    72	    if (conditions.includes(key)) {
    73	      throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);
    74	    }
    75	    if (v === null || typeof v === 'string' || typeof v === 'number') {
    76	      continue;
    77	    }
    78	    if (Array.isArray(v)) {
    79	      for (const vv of v) {
    80	        if (vv === null || typeof vv === 'string' || typeof vv === 'number') {
    81	          continue;
    82	        }
    83	        throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
    84	      }
    85	      continue;
    86	    }
    87	    if (isPlainObject(v)) {
    88	      validateConditionalStyles(v, [...conditions, key]);
    89	      continue;
    90	    }
    91	    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
    92	  }
    93	}

    11	  RawStyles,
    12	  InjectableStyle,
    13	  StyleXOptions,
    14	  FlatCompiledStyles,
    15	} from './common-types';
    16	import type { ComputedStyle, IPreRule } from './preprocess-rules/PreRule';

    18	import { createShortHash } from './hash';
    19	import { defaultOptions } from './utils/default-options';
    20	import { flattenRawStyleObject } from './preprocess-rules/flatten-raw-style-obj';
    21	import { validateNamespace } from './preprocess-rules/basic-validation';
    22	
    23	type TPropTuple = [+key: string, +styles: $ReadOnlyArray<ComputedStyle>];
    24	
    25	type ClassPathsInNamespace = {
    26	  +[className: string]: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    27	};
    28	
    29	type TClassNameTuples = $NonMaybeType<ComputedStyle>;
    30	
    31	// This takes the object of styles passed to `stylex.create` and transforms it.
    32	//   The transformation replaces style values with classNames.
    33	//
    34	// It also collects all injected styles along the way.
    35	// It then returns a tuple of the transformed style Object and an object of injected styles.
    36	//
    37	// This function does some basic validation, and then uses `styleXCreateNamespace` to transform
    38	// each namespace within,
    39	//
    40	// Before returning, it ensures that there are no duplicate styles being injected.
    41	export default function styleXCreateSet(
    42	  namespaces: { +[string]: RawStyles },
    43	  options?: StyleXOptions = defaultOptions,
    44	): [
    45	  { [string]: FlatCompiledStyles },
    46	  { [string]: InjectableStyle },
    47	  { +[string]: ClassPathsInNamespace },
    48	] {
    49	  const resolvedNamespaces: { [string]: FlatCompiledStyles } = {};
    50	  const injectedStyles: { [string]: InjectableStyle } = {};
    51	  const namespaceToClassPaths: { [string]: ClassPathsInNamespace } = {};
    52	
    53	  for (const namespaceName of Object.keys(namespaces)) {
    54	    const namespace = namespaces[namespaceName];
    55	    const classPathsInNamespace: { [string]: $ReadOnlyArray<string> } = {};
    56	
    57	    validateNamespace(namespace);
    58	
    59	    // filterReverse to remove duplicate keys and keep the last one always.
    60	    // This is the same behaviour as Object.fromEntries, except it maintains
    61	    // order correctly and is more efficient.
    62	    const seenProperties = new Set<string>();
    63	    const flattenedNamespace: $ReadOnlyArray<$ReadOnly<[string, IPreRule]>> =
    64	      flattenRawStyleObject(namespace, options).reduceRight(
    65	        (arr, curr) => {
    66	          if (seenProperties.has(curr[0])) {
    67	            return arr;
    68	          }
    69	          seenProperties.add(curr[0]);
    70	          arr.unshift(curr);
    71	          return arr;
    72	        },
    73	        [] as Array<$ReadOnly<[string, IPreRule]>>,
    74	      );
    75	
    76	    const compiledNamespaceTuples: $ReadOnlyArray<TPropTuple> =
    77	      flattenedNamespace.map(([key, value]) => {
    78	        // Skip variables-as-keys to avoid regression to dynamic styles output
    79	        if (options.enableMinifiedKeys === true && !key.startsWith('--')) {
    80	          const hashedKey = createShortHash('<>' + key);
    81	          const displayKey =
    82	            options.debug === true ? `${key}-k${hashedKey}` : `k${hashedKey}`;
    83	          return [displayKey, value.compiled(options)];
    84	        } else {
    85	          return [key, value.compiled(options)];
    86	        }
    87	      });
    88	
    89	    const namespaceObj: {
    90	      [string]: null | string,
    91	    } = {};
    92	    for (const [key, value] of compiledNamespaceTuples) {
    93	      // Remove nulls
    94	      const classNameTuples: $ReadOnlyArray<TClassNameTuples> = value
    95	        .map((v) => (Array.isArray(v) ? v : null))
    96	        .filter(Boolean);
    97	
    98	      classNameTuples.forEach(([_className, _, classesToOriginalPath]) => {
    99	        Object.assign(classPathsInNamespace, classesToOriginalPath);
   100	      });
   101	
   102	      const classNames = classNameTuples.map(([className]) => className);
   103	      const uniqueClassNames = new Set(classNames);
   104	      const className = Array.from(uniqueClassNames).join(' ');
   105	      namespaceObj[key] = className !== '' ? className : null;
   106	
   107	      for (const [className, injectable] of classNameTuples) {
   108	        if (injectedStyles[className] == null) {
   109	          injectedStyles[className] = injectable;
   110	        }
   111	      }
   112	    }
   113	    resolvedNamespaces[namespaceName] = { ...namespaceObj, $$css: true };
   114	    namespaceToClassPaths[namespaceName] = classPathsInNamespace;
   115	  }
   116	
   117	  return [resolvedNamespaces, injectedStyles, namespaceToClassPaths];
   118	}

     1	/**
     2	 * Copyright (c) Meta Platforms, Inc. and affiliates.
     3	 *
     4	 * This source code is licensed under the MIT license found in the
     5	 * LICENSE file in the root directory of this source tree.

     9	
    10	import type { RawStyles, StyleXOptions, TStyleValue } from '../common-types';
    11	
    12	import flatMapExpandedShorthands from './index';
    13	import { lastMediaQueryWinsTransform } from 'style-value-parser';
    14	import * as messages from '../messages';
    15	
    16	import {
    17	  NullPreRule,
    18	  PreRule,
    19	  PreRuleSet,
    20	  type AnyPreRule,
    21	  type IPreRule,
    22	} from './PreRule';
    23	
    24	export function flattenRawStyleObject(
    25	  style: RawStyles,
    26	  options: StyleXOptions,
    27	): $ReadOnlyArray<$ReadOnly<[string, IPreRule]>> {
    28	  let processedStyle = style;
    29	  try {
    30	    processedStyle = options.enableMediaQueryOrder
    31	      ? lastMediaQueryWinsTransform(style)
    32	      : style;
    33	  } catch (error) {
    34	    throw new Error(messages.INVALID_MEDIA_QUERY_SYNTAX);
    35	  }
    36	  return _flattenRawStyleObject(processedStyle, [], options);
    37	}
    38	
    39	export function _flattenRawStyleObject(
    40	  style: RawStyles,
    41	  keyPath: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    42	  options: StyleXOptions,
    43	): Array<$ReadOnly<[string, AnyPreRule]>> {
    44	  const flattened: Array<$ReadOnly<[string, AnyPreRule]>> = [];
    45	  for (const _key in style) {
    46	    const value = style[_key];
    47	    const key: string = _key.match(/var\(--[a-z0-9]+\)/)
    48	      ? _key.slice(4, -1)
    49	      : _key;
    50	
    51	    // Default styles
    52	    if (
    53	      value === null ||
    54	      typeof value === 'string' ||
    55	      typeof value === 'number'
    56	    ) {
    57	      const pairs: $ReadOnlyArray<[string, TStyleValue]> =
    58	        flatMapExpandedShorthands([key, value], options);
    59	      for (const [property, value] of pairs) {
    60	        if (value === null) {
    61	          flattened.push([property, new NullPreRule()]);
    62	        } else {
    63	          flattened.push([
    64	            property,
    65	            new PreRule(
    66	              property,
    67	              value,
    68	              keyPath.includes(key)
    69	                ? keyPath.map((k) => (k === key ? property : k))
    70	                : [...keyPath, property],
    71	            ),
    72	          ]);
    73	        }
    74	      }
    75	      continue;
    76	    }
    77	
    78	    // Fallback Styles
    79	    if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    80	      // Step 1: Expand properties to its constituent parts
    81	      // Collect the various values for each value in the array
    82	      // that belongs to the same property.
    83	      const equivalentPairs: {
    84	        [string]: Array<null | string | number>,
    85	      } = {};
    86	      for (const eachVal of value) {
    87	        const pairs = flatMapExpandedShorthands([key, eachVal], options);
    88	        for (const [property, val] of pairs) {
    89	          if (Array.isArray(val)) {
    90	            if (equivalentPairs[property] == null) {
    91	              equivalentPairs[property] = [...val];
    92	            } else {
    93	              equivalentPairs[property].push(...val);
    94	            }
    95	          } else if (equivalentPairs[property] == null) {
    96	            equivalentPairs[property] = [val];
    97	          } else {
    98	            equivalentPairs[property].push(val);
    99	          }
   100	        }
   101	      }
   102	      // Deduplicate
   103	      Object.entries(equivalentPairs)
   104	        // Remove Nulls
   105	        .map(([property, values]) => [
   106	          property,
   107	          [...new Set(values.filter(Boolean))],
   108	        ])
   109	        // Deduplicate and default to null when no values are found
   110	        .map(([property, values]) => [
   111	          property,
   112	          values.length === 0 ? null : values.length === 1 ? values[0] : values,
   113	        ])
   114	        // Push to flattened
   115	        .forEach(([property, value]) => {
   116	          if (value === null) {
   117	            flattened.push([property, new NullPreRule()]);
   118	          } else {
   119	            flattened.push([
   120	              property,
   121	              new PreRule(
   122	                property,
   123	                value,
   124	                keyPath.includes(_key)
   125	                  ? keyPath.map((k) => (k === _key ? property : k))
   126	                  : [...keyPath, property],
   127	              ),
   128	            ]);
   129	          }
   130	        });
   131	      continue;
   132	    }
   133	
   134	    // Object Values for properties. e.g. { color: { hover: 'red', default: 'blue' } }
   135	    if (
   136	      typeof value === 'object' &&
   137	      !key.startsWith(':') &&
   138	      !key.startsWith('@')
   139	    ) {
   140	      const equivalentPairs: { [string]: { [string]: AnyPreRule } } = {};
   141	      for (const condition in value) {
   142	        const innerValue = value[condition];
   143	
   144	        const pairs = _flattenRawStyleObject(
   145	          { [key]: innerValue },
   146	          keyPath.length > 0 ? [...keyPath, condition] : [key, condition],
   147	          options,
   148	        );
   149	        for (const [property, preRule] of pairs) {
   150	          if (equivalentPairs[property] == null) {
   151	            equivalentPairs[property] = { [condition]: preRule };
   152	          } else {
   153	            equivalentPairs[property][condition] = preRule;
   154	          }
   155	        }
   156	      }
   157	      for (const [property, obj] of Object.entries(equivalentPairs)) {
   158	        const sortedKeys = Object.keys(obj); //.sort();
   159	        const rules: Array<AnyPreRule> = [];
   160	        for (const condition of sortedKeys) {
   161	          rules.push(obj[condition]);
   162	        }
   163	        // If there are many conditions with `null` values, we will collapse them into a single `null` value.
   164	        // `PreRuleSet.create` takes care of that for us.
   165	        flattened.push([property, PreRuleSet.create(rules)]);
   166	      }
   167	    }
   168	
   169	    // Object Values for pseudos and at-rules. e.g. { ':hover': { color: 'red' } }
   170	    if (
   171	      typeof value === 'object' &&
   172	      (key.startsWith(':') || key.startsWith('@'))
   173	    ) {
   174	      const pairs = _flattenRawStyleObject(value, [...keyPath, _key], options);
   175	      for (const [property, preRule] of pairs) {
   176	        flattened.push([key + '_' + property, preRule]);
   177	      }
   178	    }
   179	  }
   180	  return flattened;
   181	}

    36	function isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr: t.Expression): boolean {
    37	  if (t.isTemplateLiteral(expr)) return true;
    38	
    39	  if (
    40	    t.isStringLiteral(expr) ||
    41	    t.isNumericLiteral(expr) ||
    42	    t.isBooleanLiteral(expr)
    43	  )
    44	    return true;
    45	
    46	  if (t.isBinaryExpression(expr)) {
    47	    return ['+', '-', '*', '/', '%', '**'].includes(expr.operator);
    48	  }
    49	
    50	  if (t.isUnaryExpression(expr)) {
    51	    return ['-', '+'].includes(expr.operator);
    52	  }
    53	
    54	  if (t.isConditionalExpression(expr)) {
    55	    return (
    56	      isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.consequent) &&
    57	      isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.alternate)
    58	    );
    59	  }
    60	
    61	  if (t.isLogicalExpression(expr)) {
    62	    if (expr.operator === '??' || expr.operator === '||') {
    63	      return (
    64	        isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.left) || isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.right)
    65	      );
    66	    }
    67	    if (expr.operator === '&&') {
    68	      return (
    69	        isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.left) && isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.right)
    70	      );
    71	    }
    72	  }
    73	
    74	  return false;
    75	}

    77	/// This function looks for `stylex.create` calls and transforms them.
    78	/// 1. It finds the first argument to `stylex.create` and validates it.
    79	/// 2. It pre-processes valid-dynamic parts of style object such as custom presets (spreads)
    80	/// 3. It evaluates the style object to get a JS object. This also handles local constants automatically.
    81	/// 4. It uses the `stylexCreate` from `@stylexjs/shared` to transform the JS
    82	///    object and to get a list of injected styles.
    83	/// 5. It converts the resulting Object back into an AST and replaces the call with it.
    84	/// 6. It also inserts `stylex.inject` calls above the current statement as needed.

   261	            const [params, inlineStyles] = fns[key];

   264

   270

   275	            }> = Object.entries(inlineStyles).map(([_key, v]) => ({
   276	              expression: v.originalExpression,
   277	              key: v.path

   283	                )

   289	              dynamicStyles = legacyExpandShorthands(dynamicStyles);

   292	            if (t.isObjectExpression(prop.value)) {
   293	              const value: t.ObjectExpression = prop.value;
   294

   296	                t.booleanLiteral(true);
   297	
   298	              const staticProps: Array<t.ObjectProperty> = [];
   299	
   300	              const conditionalProps: Array<t.ObjectProperty> = [];

   302	              value.properties.forEach((prop) => {
   303	                if (!t.isObjectProperty(prop) || t.isPrivateName(prop.key)) {
   304	                  return;
   305	                }
   306	
   307	                const objProp: t.ObjectProperty = prop;
   308	                const propKey =
   309	                  t.isIdentifier(objProp.key) && !objProp.computed
   310	                    ? objProp.key.name
   311	                    : t.isStringLiteral(objProp.key)
   312	                      ? objProp.key.value
   313	                      : null;
   314	
   315	                if (propKey == null) {
   316	                  staticProps.push(objProp);
   317	                  return;
   318	                }
   319	
   320	                if (propKey === '$$css') {
   321	                  cssTagValue = objProp.value;
   322	                  return;
   323	                }
   324	
   325	                const classList = t.isStringLiteral(objProp.value)
   326	                  ? objProp.value.value.split(' ')

   330	                const exprList: t.Expression[] = [];

   332	                classList.forEach((cls, index) => {

   334	                    ({ path }) => origClassPaths[cls] === path,
   335	                  )?.expression;

   346	                        expr,
   347	                      ),
   348	                    );
   349	                  } else {
   350	                    exprList.push(t.stringLiteral(clsWithSpace));
   351	                  }
   352	                });
   353	
   354	                const joined =
   355	                  exprList.length === 0
   356	                    ? t.stringLiteral('')
   357	                    : exprList.reduce((acc, curr) =>
   358	                        t.binaryExpression('+', acc, curr),
   359	                      );

   362	                  staticProps.push(t.objectProperty(objProp.key, joined));
   363	                } else {
   364	                  conditionalProps.push(t.objectProperty(objProp.key, joined));
   365	                }
   366	              });
   367	
   368	              let staticObj = null;
   369	              let conditionalObj = null;
   370	
   371	              if (staticProps.length > 0) {

   376	              }
   377	
   378	              if (conditionalProps.length > 0) {
   379	                conditionalProps.push(
   380	                  t.objectProperty(t.identifier('$$css'), cssTagValue),
   381	                );
   382	                conditionalObj = t.objectExpression(conditionalProps);
   383	              }
   384	
   385	              let finalFnValue: t.Expression = t.objectExpression(
   386	                Object.entries(inlineStyles).map(([key, val]) =>
   387	                  t.objectProperty(t.stringLiteral(key), val.expression),
   388	                ),
   389	              );
   390	              if (staticObj != null || conditionalObj != null) {
   391	                finalFnValue = t.arrayExpression(
   392	                  [
   393	                    staticObj && hoistExpression(path, staticObj),
   394	                    conditionalObj,
   395	                    finalFnValue,
   396	                  ].filter(Boolean),
   397	                );
   398	              }
   399	
   400	              prop.value = t.arrowFunctionExpression(params, finalFnValue);
   401	            }
   402	          }
   403	        }
   404	
   405	        return prop;
   406	      });
   407	    }
   408	
   409	    const listOfStyles = Object.entries(injectedStyles).map(
   410	      ([key, { priority, ...rest }]) => [key, rest, priority],
   411	    );
   412	
   413	    state.registerStyles(listOfStyles, path);

   416	
   417	    if (Object.keys(injectedStyles).length === 0) {
   418	      return;
   419	    }
   420	  }
   421	  state.inStyleXCreate = false;
   422	}

   424	// Validates the first argument to `stylex.create`.
   425	function validateStyleXCreate(path: NodePath<t.CallExpression>) {
   426	  if (path.parentPath == null || path.parentPath.isExpressionStatement()) {
   427	    throw path.buildCodeFrameError(
   428	      messages.unboundCallValue('create'),
   429	      SyntaxError,
   430	    );
   431	  }
   432	
   433	  if (path.node.arguments.length !== 1) {
   434	    throw path.buildCodeFrameError(
   435	      messages.illegalArgumentLength('create', 1),
   436	      SyntaxError,
   437	    );
   438	  }
   439	
   440	  const arg = path.node.arguments[0];
   441	  if (arg.type !== 'ObjectExpression') {
   442	    throw path.buildCodeFrameError(
   443	      messages.nonStyleObject('create'),
   444	      SyntaxError,
   445	    );
   446	  }
   447	
   448	  const hasSpread = arg.properties.some((prop) => t.isSpreadElement(prop));
   449	  if (hasSpread) {
   450	    throw path.buildCodeFrameError(messages.NO_OBJECT_SPREADS, SyntaxError);
   451	  }
   452	}
   453	
   454	function legacyExpandShorthands(
   455	  dynamicStyles: $ReadOnlyArray<{
   456	    +expression: t.Expression,
   457	    +key: string,
   458	    path: string,
   459	  }>,
   460	): $ReadOnlyArray<{
   461	  +expression: t.Expression,
   462	  +key: string,
   463	  path: string,
   464	}> {
   465	  const expandedKeysToKeyPaths = dynamicStyles
   466	    .flatMap(({ key }, i) => {
   467	      return flatMapExpandedShorthands([key, 'p' + i], {
   468	        styleResolution: 'legacy-expand-shorthands',
   469	      });
   470	    })
   471	    .map(([key, value]) => {
   472	      if (typeof value !== 'string') {
   473	        return null;
   474	      }
   475	      const index = parseInt(value.slice(1), 10);
   476	      const thatDynStyle = dynamicStyles[index];
   477	      return {
   478	        ...thatDynStyle,
   479	        key,
   480	        path:
   481	          thatDynStyle.path === thatDynStyle.key
   482	            ? key
   483	            : thatDynStyle.path.includes(thatDynStyle.key + '_')
   484	              ? thatDynStyle.path.replace(thatDynStyle.key + '_', key + '_')
   485	              : thatDynStyle.path.replace('_' + thatDynStyle.key, '_' + key),
   486	      };
   487	    })
   488	    .filter(Boolean);
   489	
   490	  return expandedKeysToKeyPaths;
   491	}

     1	/**
     2	 * Copyright (c) Meta Platforms, Inc. and affiliates.

    10	/* eslint-disable no-unused-vars */
    11	import type { NodePath } from '@babel/traverse';
    12	import type { FunctionConfig } from '../utils/evaluate-path';
    13	
    14	import * as t from '@babel/types';
    15	import StateManager from '../utils/state-manager';
    16	import { evaluate } from '../utils/evaluate-path';
    17	import { create, utils } from '../shared';
    18	import { messages } from '../shared';
    19	import {
    20	  timeUnits,
    21	  lengthUnits,
    22	  getNumberSuffix,
    23	} from '../shared/utils/transform-value';
    24	
    25	type TInlineStyles = {
    26	  [string]: {
    27	    +path: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    28	    +originalExpression: t.Expression,
    29	    +expression: t.Expression | t.PatternLike,
    30	  },
    31	};
    32	
    33	type DynamicFns = {
    34	  [string]: [
    35	    +params: Array<t.Identifier>,
    36	    +inlineStyles: $ReadOnly<TInlineStyles>,
    37	  ],
    38	};
    39	
    40	// This
    41	export function evaluateStyleXCreateArg(
    42	  path: NodePath<>,
    43	  traversalState: StateManager,
    44	  functions: FunctionConfig = { identifiers: {}, memberExpressions: {} },
    45	): $ReadOnly<{
    46	  confident: boolean,
    47	  value: any,
    48	  deopt?: null | NodePath<>,
    49	  reason?: string,
    50	  fns?: DynamicFns,
    51	}> {
    52	  if (!path.isObjectExpression()) {
    53	    return evaluate(path, traversalState, functions);
    54	  }
    55	
    56	  const value: { [string]: mixed } = {};
    57	  const fns: DynamicFns = {};
    58	
    59	  for (const prop of path.get('properties')) {
    60	    if (!prop.isObjectProperty()) {
    61	      return evaluate(path, traversalState, functions);
    62	    }
    63	    const objPropPath: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty> = prop;
    64	    const keyResult = evaluateObjKey(objPropPath, traversalState, functions);
    65	    if (!keyResult.confident) {
    66	      return { confident: false, deopt: keyResult.deopt, value: null };
    67	    }
    68	    const key = keyResult.value;
    69	
    70	    const valPath = prop.get('value');
    71	    if (!valPath.isArrowFunctionExpression()) {
    72	      const val = evaluate(valPath, traversalState, functions);
    73	      if (!val.confident) {
    74	        return val;
    75	      }
    76	      value[key] = val.value;
    77	      continue;
    78	    }
    79	    const fnPath: NodePath<t.ArrowFunctionExpression> = valPath;
    80	    const allParams: Array<
    81	      NodePath<t.Identifier | t.SpreadElement | t.Pattern>,
    82	    > = fnPath.get('params');
    83	
    84	    validateDynamicStyleParams(fnPath, allParams);
    85	
    86	    const params: Array<t.Identifier> = allParams
    87	      .filter(
    88	        (
    89	          param: NodePath<t.Identifier | t.Pattern | t.SpreadElement>,
    90	        ): param is NodePath<t.Identifier> => param.isIdentifier(),
    91	      )
    92	      .map((param) => param.node);
    93	
    94	    const fnBody = fnPath.get('body');
    95	    if (!fnBody.isObjectExpression()) {
    96	      // We only allow arrow functions without block bodies.
    97	      return evaluate(path, traversalState, functions);
    98	    }
    99	    const fnObjectBody: NodePath<t.ObjectExpression> = fnBody;
   100	    const evalResult = evaluatePartialObjectRecursively(
   101	      fnObjectBody,
   102	      traversalState,
   103	      functions,
   104	    );
   105	
   106	    if (!evalResult.confident) {
   107	      const { confident, value: v, deopt } = evalResult;
   108	      return { confident, value: v, deopt };
   109	    }
   110	    const { value: v, inlineStyles } = evalResult;
   111	    value[key] = v;
   112	    fns[key] = [params, inlineStyles ?? {}];
   113	  }
   114	
   115	  return { value, confident: true, fns };
   116	}
   117	
   118	function evaluatePartialObjectRecursively(
   119	  path: NodePath<t.ObjectExpression>,
   120	  traversalState: StateManager,
   121	  functions: FunctionConfig = { identifiers: {}, memberExpressions: {} },
   122	  keyPath: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
   123	): $ReadOnly<{
   124	  confident: boolean,
   125	  value: any,
   126	  deopt?: null | NodePath<>,
   127	  reason?: string,
   128	  inlineStyles?: $ReadOnly<TInlineStyles>,
   129	}> {
   130	  const obj: { [string]: mixed } = {};
   131	  const inlineStyles: TInlineStyles = {};
   132	  const props: $ReadOnlyArray<
   133	    NodePath<t.ObjectMethod | t.ObjectProperty | t.SpreadElement>,
   134	  > = path.get('properties');
   135	  for (const prop of props) {
   136	    if (prop.isObjectMethod()) {
   137	      return { value: null, confident: false };
   138	    }
   139	    if (prop.isSpreadElement()) {
   140	      const result = evaluate(prop.get('argument'), traversalState, functions);
   141	      if (!result.confident) {
   142	        return result;
   143	      }
   144	      Object.assign(obj, result.value);
   145	      continue;
   146	    }
   147	    if (prop.isObjectProperty()) {
   148	      const keyResult = evaluateObjKey(prop, traversalState, functions);
   149	      if (!keyResult.confident) {
   150	        return { confident: false, deopt: keyResult.deopt, value: null };
   151	      }
   152	      let key = keyResult.value;
   153	      if (key.startsWith('var(') && key.endsWith(')')) {
   154	        key = key.slice(4, -1);
   155	      }
   156	
   157	      const valuePath: NodePath<t.Expression | t.PatternLike> =
   158	        prop.get('value');
   159	
   160	      if (valuePath.isObjectExpression()) {
   161	        const result = evaluatePartialObjectRecursively(
   162	          valuePath,
   163	          traversalState,
   164	          functions,
   165	          [...keyPath, key],
   166	        );
   167	        if (!result.confident) {
   168	          return { confident: false, deopt: result.deopt, value: null };
   169	        }
   170	        obj[key] = result.value;
   171	        Object.assign(inlineStyles, result.inlineStyles);
   172	      } else {
   173	        const result = evaluate(valuePath, traversalState, functions);
   174	        if (!result.confident) {
   175	          const fullKeyPath = [...keyPath, key];
   176	          const varName =
   177	            '--x-' +
   178	            (keyPath.length > 0
   179	              ? utils.hash([...keyPath, key].join('_'))
   180	              : key);
   181	          obj[key] = `var(${varName})`;
   182	          const node = valuePath.node;
   183	          if (!t.isExpression(node)) {
   184	            throw valuePath.buildCodeFrameError(
   185	              'Expected expression as style value',
   186	              SyntaxError,
   187	            );
   188	          }
   189	          const expression: t.Expression = node as $FlowFixMe;
   190	
   191	          const propName =
   192	            fullKeyPath.find(
   193	              (k) =>
   194	                !k.startsWith(':') && !k.startsWith('@') && k !== 'default',
   195	            ) ?? key;
   196	
   197	          const unit =
   198	            timeUnits.has(propName) || lengthUnits.has(propName)
   199	              ? getNumberSuffix(propName)
   200	              : '';
   201	
   202	          const inlineStyleExpression =
   203	            unit !== ''
   204	              ? t.callExpression(
   205	                  t.arrowFunctionExpression(
   206	                    [t.identifier('val')],
   207	                    t.conditionalExpression(
   208	                      t.binaryExpression(
   209	                        '===',
   210	                        t.unaryExpression('typeof', t.identifier('val')),
   211	                        t.stringLiteral('number'),
   212	                      ),
   213	                      t.binaryExpression(
   214	                        '+',
   215	                        t.identifier('val'),
   216	                        t.stringLiteral(unit),
   217	                      ),
   218	                      t.conditionalExpression(
   219	                        t.binaryExpression(
   220	                          '!=',
   221	                          t.identifier('val'),
   222	                          t.nullLiteral(),
   223	                        ),
   224	                        t.identifier('val'),
   225	                        t.identifier('undefined'),
   226	                      ),
   227	                    ),
   228	                  ),
   229	                  [expression as t.Expression],
   230	                )
   231	              : t.conditionalExpression(
   232	                  t.binaryExpression('!=', expression, t.nullLiteral()),
   233	                  expression,
   234	                  t.identifier('undefined'),
   235	                );
   236	          inlineStyles[varName] = {
   237	            path: [...keyPath, key],
   238	            originalExpression: expression,
   239	            expression: inlineStyleExpression,
   240	          };
   241	        } else {
   242	          obj[key] = result.value;
   243	        }
   244	      }
   245	    }
   246	  }
   247	  return { value: obj, confident: true, inlineStyles };
   248	}
   249	
   250	type KeyResult =
   251	  | { confident: true, value: string }
   252	  | { confident: false, deopt?: null | NodePath<> };
   253	
   254	function evaluateObjKey(
   255	  prop: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty>,
   256	  traversalState: StateManager,
   257	  functions: FunctionConfig,
   258	): KeyResult {
   259	  const keyPath: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty['key']> = prop.get('key');
   260	  let key: string;
   261	  if ((prop.node as t.ObjectProperty).computed) {
   262	    const result = evaluate(keyPath, traversalState, functions);
   263	    if (!result.confident) {
   264	      return { confident: false, deopt: result.deopt };
   265	    }
   266	    key = result.value;
   267	  } else if (keyPath.isIdentifier()) {
   268	    key = keyPath.node.name;
   269	  } else {
   270	    // TODO: This is'nt handling all possible types that `keyPath` could be
   271	    key = (keyPath.node as $FlowFixMe).value;
   272	  }
   273	  return {
   274	    confident: true,
   275	    value: String(key),
   276	  };
   277	}
   278	
   279	function validateDynamicStyleParams(
   280	  path: NodePath<t.ArrowFunctionExpression>,
   281	  params: Array<NodePath<t.Identifier | t.SpreadElement | t.Pattern>>,
   282	) {
   283	  if (params.some((param) => !param.isIdentifier())) {
   284	    throw path.buildCodeFrameError(
   285	      messages.ONLY_NAMED_PARAMETERS_IN_DYNAMIC_STYLE_FUNCTIONS,
   286	      SyntaxError,
   287	    );
   288	  }
   289	}
   290

const { transformSync } = require('@babel/core');
const stylexPlugin = require('./packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/src/index');

function transformWithInlineConsts(source, opts = {}) {
  try {
    const { code, metadata } = transformSync(source, {
      filename: path.join(__dirname, '__tests__/__fixtures__/main.stylex.js'),
      parserOpts: { sourceType: 'module' },
      babelrc: false,
      plugins: [
        [
          stylexPlugin,
          {
            ...opts,
            unstable_moduleResolution: {
              rootDir: path.join(__dirname, 'packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/__fixtures__'),
              type: 'commonJS',
            },
          },
        ],
      ],
    });
    return { code, metadata };
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('ERROR:', e.message);
    return { code: null, metadata: null };
  }
}

  import * as stylex from '@stylexjs/stylex';

      transition: {

      },
    }),
  });
\`);

console.log('Code:', result.code);

const path = require('path');
const { transformSync } = require('@babel/core');
const stylexPlugin = require('./packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/lib/index');

function transformWithInlineConsts(source, opts = {}) {
  try {
    const { code, metadata } = transformSync(source, {
      filename: path.join(__dirname, 'packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/__fixtures__/main.stylex.js'),
      parserOpts: { sourceType: 'module' },
      babelrc: false,
      plugins: [
        [
          stylexPlugin.default || stylexPlugin,
          {
            ...opts,
            unstable_moduleResolution: {
              rootDir: path.join(__dirname, 'packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/__fixtures__'),
              type: 'commonJS',
            },
          },
        ],
      ],
    });
    return { code, metadata };
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('ERROR:', e.message);
    if (e.stack) console.error(e.stack);
    return { code: null, metadata: null };
  }
}

const result = transformWithInlineConsts(`
  import * as stylex from '@stylexjs/stylex';

`);

Great, I've reproduced the error. Now let me understand the issue more deeply.

The error is in `validateConditionalStyles` in `basic-validation.js`. The issue is that when using dynamic styles with constants from `defineConsts`, the constants are inlined as `var(--...)` placeholders. But the validation function checks if a key starts with `@`, `:`, `var(--`, or is `'default'`. 

Let me trace through the flow:

1. The user writes: 
```js
stylex.create({
  nodeEnd: (animationDuration) => ({
    transition: {
      [breakpoints.small]: 'none',
      default: `transform ${animationDuration}ms ease-in-out`,
    },
  }),
});
```

2. `breakpoints.small` is a constant that gets inlined. Let me check what value it gets inlined to. Looking at the constants file, `breakpoints.small = '@media (max-width: 600px)'`. When this is used in `stylex.create`, it gets replaced with `var(--x1r2wpmh)` (a CSS variable placeholder).

3. The evaluation of the dynamic function happens in `evaluatePartialObjectRecursively`. For the computed property `[breakpoints.small]`, it evaluates to the inlined constant value (which is like `var(--x1r2wpmh)` or some hash). Let me check how constants are inlined.

     9	
    10	import type { InjectableConstStyle, StyleXOptions } from './common-types';
    11	import type { ConstsConfig } from './stylex-consts-utils';
    12	
    13	import { defaultOptions } from './utils/default-options';
    14	import * as messages from './messages';
    15	
    16	import createHash from './hash';
    17	
    18	export default function styleXDefineConsts<Vars: ConstsConfig>(
    19	  constants: Vars,
    20	  options: $ReadOnly<{ ...Partial<StyleXOptions>, exportId: string, ... }>,
    21	): [
    22	  { [string]: string | number }, // jsOutput JS output
    23	  { [string]: InjectableConstStyle }, // metadata for registerinjectableStyles
    24	] {
    25	  const { classNamePrefix, exportId, debug, enableDebugClassNames } = {
    26	    ...defaultOptions,
    27	    ...options,
    28	  };
    29	
    30	  const jsOutput: { [string]: string | number } = {};
    31	  const injectableStyles: { [string]: InjectableConstStyle } = {};
    32	
    33	  for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(constants)) {
    34	    if (key.startsWith('--')) {
    35	      throw new Error(messages.INVALID_CONST_KEY);
    36	    }
    37	
    38	    const varSafeKey = (
    39	      key[0] >= '0' && key[0] <= '9' ? `_${key}` : key
    40	    ).replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, '_');
    41	
    42	    const constKey =
    43	      debug && enableDebugClassNames
    44	        ? `${varSafeKey}-${classNamePrefix}${createHash(`${exportId}.${key}`)}`
    45	        : `${classNamePrefix}${createHash(`${exportId}.${key}`)}`;
    46	
    47	    jsOutput[key] = value;
    48	    injectableStyles[constKey] = {
    49	      constKey,
    50	      constVal: value,
    51	      priority: 0,
    52	      ltr: '',
    53	      rtl: null,
    54	    };
    55	  }
    56	
    57	  return [jsOutput, injectableStyles];
    58	}

     1	/**

     9	
    10	/**
    11	 * This is a extended version of the path evaluation code from Babel.
    12	 *
    13	 * The original can be found at:
    14	 * https://github.com/babel/babel/blob/main/packages/babel-traverse/src/path/evaluation.ts
    15	 *
    16	 * The following extensions were made:
    17	 * - It can accept a mapping from variable names to functions
    18	 *   which when encountered will be evaluated instead of deopting.
    19	 *   - The functions can be configured to accept the raw path instead of
    20	 *     static values to handle dynamic values.
    21	 * - It can handle object spreads when the spread value itself is statically evaluated.
    22	 */
    23	
    24	import type { NodePath, Binding } from '@babel/traverse';
    25	
    26	import { parseSync } from '@babel/core';
    27	import traverse from '@babel/traverse';
    28	import * as t from '@babel/types';
    29	import StateManager from './state-manager';
    30	import { utils } from '../shared';
    31	import * as errMsgs from './evaluation-errors';
    32	
    33	// This file contains Babels metainterpreter that can evaluate static code.
    34	
    35	const VALID_CALLEES = ['String', 'Number', 'Math', 'Object', 'Array'];
    36	const INVALID_METHODS = [
    37	  'random',
    38	  'assign',
    39	  'defineProperties',
    40	  'defineProperty',
    41	  'freeze',
    42	  'seal',
    43	  'splice',
    44	];
    45	
    46	function isValidCallee(val: string): boolean {
    47	  return (VALID_CALLEES as $ReadOnlyArray<string>).includes(val);
    48	}
    49	
    50	function isInvalidMethod(val: string): boolean {
    51	  return INVALID_METHODS.includes(val);
    52	}
    53	
    54	export type FunctionConfig = {
    55	  identifiers: {
    56	    [fnName: string]: $FlowFixMe,
    57	  },
    58	  memberExpressions: {
    59	    [key: string]: {
    60	      [memberName: string]: {
    61	        fn: (...args: $FlowFixMe[]) => $FlowFixMe,
    62	        takesPath?: boolean,
    63	      },
    64	    },
    65	  },
    66	};
    67	
    68	type State = {
    69	  confident: boolean,
    70	  deoptPath: NodePath<> | null,
    71	  deoptReason?: string,
    72	  seen: Map<t.Node, Result>,
    73	  addedImports: Set<string>,
    74	  functions: FunctionConfig,
    75	  traversalState: StateManager,
    76	};
    77	
    78	type Result =
    79	  | {
    80	      resolved: true,
    81	      value: any,
    82	    }
    83	  | {
    84	      resolved: false,
    85	      reason: string,
    86	    };
    87	/**
    88	 * Deopts the evaluation
    89	 */
    90	function deopt(path: NodePath<>, state: State, reason: string): void {
    91	  if (!state.confident) return;
    92	  state.deoptPath = path;
    93	  state.confident = false;
    94	  state.deoptReason = reason;
    95	}
    96	
    97	function evaluateImportedFile(
    98	  filePath: string,
    99	  namedExport: string,
   100	  state: State,
   101	  bindingPath: NodePath<>,
   102	): any {
   103	  const fs = require('fs');
   104	  const fileContents = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
   105	  // It's safe to use `.babelrc` here because we're only
   106	  // interested in the JS runtime, and not the CSS.
   107	  // TODO: in environments where `.babelrc` is not available,
   108	  // we need to find a way to decide whether to use Flow or TS syntax extensions.
   109	  const ast: null | t.File | { +errors: mixed } = parseSync(fileContents, {
   110	    babelrc: true,
   111	  });
   112	  if (!ast || ast.errors || !t.isNode(ast)) {
   113	    deopt(bindingPath, state, errMsgs.IMPORT_FILE_PARSING_ERROR);
   114	    return;
   115	  }
   116	
   117	  const astNode: t.Node = ast as $FlowFixMe;
   118	
   119	  let result: any;
   120	
   121	  traverse(astNode, {
   122	    ExportNamedDeclaration(path: NodePath<t.ExportNamedDeclaration>) {
   123	      const declaration = path.get('declaration');
   124	
   125	      if (declaration.isVariableDeclaration()) {
   126	        const decls = declaration.get('declarations');
   127	
   128	        const finder = (decl: NodePath<t.Node>) => {
   129	          if (decl.isVariableDeclarator()) {
   130	            const id = decl.get('id');
   131	            const init: ?NodePath<t.Expression> = (
   132	              decl as NodePath<t.VariableDeclarator>
   133	            ).get('init');
   134	            if (
   135	              id.isIdentifier() &&
   136	              id.node.name === namedExport &&
   137	              init != null &&
   138	              init.isExpression()
   139	            ) {
   140	              result = evaluateCached(init, state);
   141	            }
   142	          }
   143	        };
   144	        if (Array.isArray(decls)) {
   145	          decls.forEach(finder);
   146	        } else {
   147	          finder(decls);
   148	        }
   149	      }
   150	    },
   151	  });
   152	
   153	  if (state.confident) {
   154	    return result;
   155	  } else {
   156	    deopt(bindingPath, state, errMsgs.IMPORT_FILE_EVAL_ERROR);
   157	    return;
   158	  }
   159	}
   160	
   161	function evaluateThemeRef(
   162	  fileName: string,
   163	  exportName: string,
   164	  state: State,
   165	): { [key: string]: string } {
   166	  const resolveKey = (key: string) => {
   167	    if (key.startsWith('--')) {
   168	      return `var(${key})`;
   169	    }
   170	
   171	    const strToHash =
   172	      key === '__varGroupHash__'
   173	        ? utils.genFileBasedIdentifier({ fileName, exportName })
   174	        : utils.genFileBasedIdentifier({ fileName, exportName, key });
   175	
   176	    const { debug, enableDebugClassNames } = state.traversalState.options;
   177	
   178	    const varSafeKey =
   179	      key === '__varGroupHash__'
   180	        ? ''
   181	        : (key[0] >= '0' && key[0] <= '9' ? `_${key}` : key).replace(
   182	            /[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,
   183	            '_',
   184	          ) + '-';
   185	
   186	    const varName =
   187	      debug && enableDebugClassNames
   188	        ? varSafeKey +
   189	          state.traversalState.options.classNamePrefix +
   190	          utils.hash(strToHash)
   191	        : state.traversalState.options.classNamePrefix + utils.hash(strToHash);
   192	
   193	    if (key === '__varGroupHash__') {
   194	      return varName;
   195	    }
   196	    return `var(--${varName})`;
   197	  };
   198	
   199	  // A JS proxy that uses the key to generate a string value using the `resolveKey` function
   200	  const proxy = new Proxy(
   201	    {},
   202	    {
   203	      get(_, key: string) {
   204	        return resolveKey(key);
   205	      },
   206	      set(_, key: string, value: string) {
   207	        throw new Error(
   208	          `Cannot set value ${value} to key ${key} in theme ${fileName}`,
   209	        );
   210	      },
   211	    },
   212	  );
   213	
   214	  return proxy;
   215	}
   216	
   217	/**
   218	 * We wrap the _evaluate method so we can track `seen` nodes, we push an item
   219	 * to the map before we actually evaluate it so we can deopt on self recursive
   220	 * nodes such as:
   221	 *
   222	 *   var g = a ? 1 : 2,
   223	 *       a = g * this.foo
   224	 */
   225	function evaluateCached(path: NodePath<>, state: State): any {
   226	  const { node } = path;
   227	  const { seen } = state;
   228	
   229	  const existing: ?Result = seen.get(node);
   230	  if (existing != null) {
   231	    if (existing.resolved) {
   232	      return existing.value;
   233	    } else {
   234	      deopt(path, state, existing.reason);
   235	      return;
   236	    }
   237	  } else {
   238	    const item: Result = { resolved: false, reason: 'Currently evaluating' };
   239	    seen.set(node, item);
   240	
   241	    if (node == null) {
   242	      deopt(path, state, errMsgs.PATH_WITHOUT_NODE);
   243	      return;
   244	    }
   245	
   246	    const val = _evaluate(path, state);
   247	    if (state.confident) {
   248	      seen.set(node, {
   249	        resolved: true,
   250	        value: val,
   251	      });
   252	    }
   253	
   254	    return val;
   255	  }
   256	}
   257	
   258	function _evaluate(path: NodePath<>, state: State): any {
   259	  if (!state.confident) return;
   260	
   261	  if (path.isArrowFunctionExpression()) {
   262	    const body = path.get('body');
   263	    const params: $ReadOnlyArray<
   264	      NodePath<t.Identifier | t.Pattern | t.RestElement>,
   265	    > = path.get('params');
   266	    const identParams = params
   267	      .filter(
   268	        (
   269	          param: NodePath<t.Identifier | t.Pattern | t.RestElement>,
   270	        ): param is NodePath<t.Identifier> => param.isIdentifier(),
   271	      )
   272	      .map((paramPath) => paramPath.node.name);
   273	    if (body.isExpression() && identParams.length === params.length) {
   274	      const expr: NodePath<t.Expression> = body;
   275	      return (...args) => {
   276	        const identifierEntries = identParams.map(
   277	          (ident, index): [string, any] => [ident, args[index]],
   278	        );
   279	        const identifiersObj = Object.fromEntries(identifierEntries);
   280	        const result = evaluate(expr, state.traversalState, {
   281	          ...state.functions,
   282	          identifiers: { ...state.functions.identifiers, ...identifiersObj },
   283	        });
   284	        return result.value;
   285	      };
   286	    }
   287	  }
   288	
   289	  if (path.isIdentifier()) {
   290	    const name: string = path.node.name;
   291	    if (Object.keys(state.functions?.identifiers ?? {}).includes(name)) {
   292	      return state.functions.identifiers[name];
   293	    }
   294	  }
   295	
   296	  if (path.isTSAsExpression()) {
   297	    const expr: NodePath<t.Expression> = path.get('expression');
   298	    return evaluateCached(expr, state);
   299	  }
   300	
   301	  if (path.node.type === 'TSSatisfiesExpression') {
   302	    const expr: NodePath<t.Expression> = (path as $FlowFixMe).get('expression');
   303	    return evaluateCached(expr, state);
   304	  }
   305	
   306	  if (path.isSequenceExpression()) {
   307	    const exprs = path.get('expressions');
   308	    return evaluateCached(exprs[exprs.length - 1], state);
   309	  }
   310	
   311	  if (
   312	    path.isStringLiteral() ||
   313	    path.isNumericLiteral() ||
   314	    path.isBooleanLiteral()
   315	  ) {
   316	    return path.node.value;
   317	  }
   318	
   319	  if (path.isNullLiteral()) {
   320	    return null;
   321	  }
   322	
   323	  if (path.isTemplateLiteral()) {
   324	    return evaluateQuasis(path, path.node.quasis, state);
   325	  }
   326	
   327	  const maybeTag = path.isTaggedTemplateExpression() && path.get('tag');
   328	  if (
   329	    path.isTaggedTemplateExpression() &&
   330	    maybeTag &&
   331	    maybeTag.isMemberExpression()
   332	  ) {
   333	    const tag: NodePath<t.MemberExpression> = maybeTag;
   334	    const object: NodePath<t.Expression | t.Super> = tag.get('object');
   335	
   336	    if (object.isIdentifier()) {
   337	      const name = object.node.name;
   338	      const property: NodePath<> = tag.get('property');
   339	
   340	      if (
   341	        name === 'String' &&
   342	        !path.scope.hasBinding(name) &&
   343	        property.isIdentifier() &&
   344	        property.node.name === 'raw'
   345	      ) {
   346	        return evaluateQuasis(path, path.node.quasi.quasis, state, true);
   347	      }
   348	    }
   349	  }
   350	
   351	  if (path.isConditionalExpression()) {
   352	    const testResult = evaluateCached(path.get('test'), state);
   353	    if (!state.confident) return;
   354	    if (testResult) {
   355	      return evaluateCached(path.get('consequent'), state);
   356	    } else {
   357	      return evaluateCached(path.get('alternate'), state);
   358	    }
   359	  }
   360	
   361	  if (path.isExpressionWrapper()) {
   362	    // TypeCastExpression, ExpressionStatement etc
   363	    return evaluateCached(path.get('expression'), state);
   364	  }
   365	
   366	  // "foo".length
   367	  if (
   368	    path.isMemberExpression() &&
   369	    !path.parentPath.isCallExpression({ callee: path.node })
   370	  ) {
   371	    const object = evaluateCached(path.get('object'), state);
   372	    if (!state.confident) {
   373	      return;
   374	    }
   375	
   376	    const propPath = path.get('property');
   377	
   378	    let property;
   379	    if (path.node.computed) {
   380	      property = evaluateCached(propPath, state);
   381	      if (!state.confident) {
   382	        return;
   383	      }
   384	    } else if (propPath.isIdentifier()) {
   385	      property = propPath.node.name;
   386	    } else if (propPath.isStringLiteral()) {
   387	      property = propPath.node.value;
   388	    } else {
   389	      return deopt(propPath, state, errMsgs.UNEXPECTED_MEMBER_LOOKUP);
   390	    }
   391	
   392	    return object[property];
   393	  }
   394	
   395	  if (path.isReferencedIdentifier()) {
   396	    const binding: ?Binding = path.scope?.getBinding(path.node.name);
   397	
   398	    const bindingPath = binding?.path;
   399	    if (
   400	      binding &&
   401	      bindingPath &&
   402	      !bindingPath.isImportDefaultSpecifier() &&
   403	      !bindingPath.isImportNamespaceSpecifier() &&
   404	      bindingPath.isImportSpecifier()
   405	    ) {
   406	      const importSpecifierPath: NodePath<t.ImportSpecifier> = bindingPath;
   407	      const importSpecifierNode: t.ImportSpecifier = importSpecifierPath.node;
   408	      // const localName = binding.path.node.local.name;
   409	      const imported: t.Identifier | t.StringLiteral =
   410	        importSpecifierNode.imported;
   411	      const importedName =
   412	        imported.type === 'Identifier' ? imported.name : imported.value;
   413	      const importPath = binding.path.parentPath;
   414	      if (importPath && importPath.isImportDeclaration()) {
   415	        const absPath = state.traversalState.importPathResolver(
   416	          importPath.node.source.value,
   417	        );
   418	        if (!absPath) {
   419	          return deopt(
   420	            binding.path,
   421	            state,
   422	            errMsgs.IMPORT_PATH_RESOLUTION_ERROR,
   423	          );
   424	        }
   425	        const [type, value] = absPath;
   426	
   427	        const returnValue =
   428	          type === 'themeNameRef'
   429	            ? evaluateThemeRef(value, importedName, state)
   430	            : evaluateImportedFile(value, importedName, state, bindingPath);
   431	        if (state.confident) {
   432	          if (
   433	            !state.addedImports.has(importPath.node.source.value) &&
   434	            state.traversalState.treeshakeCompensation
   435	          ) {
   436	            importPath.insertBefore(
   437	              t.importDeclaration([], importPath.node.source),
   438	            );
   439	            state.addedImports.add(importPath.node.source.value);
   440	          }
   441	          return returnValue;
   442	        } else {
   443	          deopt(binding.path, state, errMsgs.IMPORT_FILE_EVAL_ERROR);
   444	        }
   445	      }
   446	    }
   447	
   448	    if (binding && bindingPath && bindingPath.isImportDefaultSpecifier()) {
   449	      deopt(binding.path, state, errMsgs.IMPORT_FILE_EVAL_ERROR);
   450	    }
   451	
   452	    if (binding && binding.constantViolations.length > 0) {
   453	      return deopt(binding.path, state, errMsgs.NON_CONSTANT);
   454	    }
   455	
   456	    if (binding && path.node.start < binding.path.node.end) {
   457	      return deopt(binding.path, state, errMsgs.USED_BEFORE_DECLARATION);
   458	    }
   459	
   460	    if (binding && binding.hasValue) {
   461	      return binding.value;
   462	    } else {
   463	      if (path.node.name === 'undefined') {
   464	        return binding
   465	          ? deopt(binding.path, state, errMsgs.UNINITIALIZED_CONST)
   466	          : undefined;
   467	      } else if (path.node.name === 'Infinity') {
   468	        return binding
   469	          ? deopt(binding.path, state, errMsgs.UNINITIALIZED_CONST)
   470	          : Infinity;
   471	      } else if (path.node.name === 'NaN') {
   472	        return binding
   473	          ? deopt(binding.path, state, errMsgs.UNINITIALIZED_CONST)
   474	          : NaN;
   475	      }
   476	
   477	      const resolved = (path as $FlowFixMe).resolve();
   478	      if (resolved === path) {
   479	        return deopt(path, state, errMsgs.UNDEFINED_CONST);
   480	      } else {
   481	        return evaluateCached(resolved, state);
   482	      }
   483	    }
   484	  }
   485	
   486	  if (path.isUnaryExpression({ prefix: true })) {
   487	    if (path.node.operator === 'void') {
   488	      // we don't need to evaluate the argument to know what this will return
   489	      return undefined;
   490	    }
   491	
   492	    const argument = path.get('argument');
   493	    if (
   494	      path.node.operator === 'typeof' &&
   495	      (argument.isFunction() || argument.isClass())
   496	    ) {
   497	      return 'function';
   498	    }
   499	
   500	    const arg = evaluateCached(argument, state);
   501	    if (!state.confident) return;
   502	    switch (path.node.operator) {
   503	      case '!':
   504	        return !arg;
   505	      case '+':
   506	        return +arg;
   507	      case '-':
   508	        return -arg;
   509	      case '~':
   510	        return ~arg;
   511	      case 'typeof':
   512	        return typeof arg;
   513	      case 'void':
   514	        return undefined;
   515	      default:
   516	        return deopt(
   517	          path,
   518	          state,
   519	          errMsgs.UNSUPPORTED_OPERATOR(path.node.operator),
   520	        );
   521	    }
   522	  }
   523	
   524	  if (path.isArrayExpression()) {
   525	    const arrPath: NodePath<t.ArrayExpression> = path;
   526	    const arr = [];
   527	    const elems: $ReadOnlyArray<NodePath<>> = arrPath.get('elements');
   528	    for (const elem of elems) {
   529	      const elemValue = evaluate(elem, state.traversalState, state.functions);
   530	
   531	      if (elemValue.confident) {
   532	        arr.push(elemValue.value);
   533	      } else {
   534	        elemValue.deopt &&
   535	          deopt(elemValue.deopt, state, elemValue.reason ?? 'unknown error');
   536	        return;
   537	      }
   538	    }
   539	    return arr;
   540	  }
   541	
   542	  if (path.isObjectExpression()) {
   543	    const obj: { [string]: mixed } = {};
   544	    const props: $ReadOnlyArray<
   545	      NodePath<t.ObjectMethod | t.ObjectProperty | t.SpreadElement>,
   546	    > = path.get('properties');
   547	    for (const prop of props) {
   548	      if (prop.isObjectMethod()) {
   549	        return deopt(prop, state, errMsgs.OBJECT_METHOD);
   550	      }
   551	      if (prop.isSpreadElement()) {
   552	        const spreadExpression = evaluateCached(prop.get('argument'), state);
   553	        if (!state.confident) {
   554	          return deopt(prop, state, state.deoptReason ?? 'unknown error');
   555	        }
   556	        Object.assign(obj, spreadExpression);
   557	        continue;
   558	      }
   559	      if (prop.isObjectProperty()) {
   560	        const keyPath: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty['key']> = prop.get('key');
   561	        let key: string | number | boolean;
   562	        if (prop.node.computed) {
   563	          const {
   564	            confident,
   565	            deopt: resultDeopt,

   340	 * This function take an Array of CSS rules, de-duplicates them, sorts them priority and generates
   341	 * a final CSS file.
   342	 *
   343	 * When Stylex is correctly configured, the babel plugin will return an array of CSS rule objects.
   344	 * You're expected to concatenate all the Rules into a single Array and use this function to convert
   345	 * that into the final CSS file.

   347	 * End-users can choose to not use this function and use their own logic instead.
   348	 */
   349	export type Rule = [

   351	  {
   352	    ltr: string,
   353	    rtl?: null | string,
   354	    constKey?: string,
   355	    constVal?: string | number,
   356	  },

   359	function processStylexRules(
   360	  rules: Array<Rule>,
   361	  useLayers: boolean = false,
   362	): string {
   363	  if (rules.length === 0) {
   364	    return '';
   365	  }
   366	
   367	  const constantRules = rules.filter(
   368	    ([, ruleObj]) => ruleObj?.constKey != null && ruleObj?.constVal != null,
   369	  );
   370	  const nonConstantRules = rules.filter(
   371	    ([, ruleObj]) => !(ruleObj?.constKey != null && ruleObj?.constVal != null),
   372	  );
   373	
   374	  const constsMap: Map<string, string | number> = new Map();
   375	  for (const [keyhash, ruleObj] of constantRules) {
   376	    // $FlowFixMe null check above
   377	    const constVal: string | number = ruleObj.constVal;
   378	    const constName = `var(--${keyhash})`;
   379	    constsMap.set(constName, constVal);
   380	  }
   381	
   382	  function resolveConstant(
   383	    value: string | number,
   384	    visited: Set<string> = new Set(),
   385	  ): string | number {
   386	    if (typeof value !== 'string') return value;
   387	    const regex = /var\((--[A-Za-z0-9_-]+)\)/g;
   388	    let result: string = value;
   389	    let match: RegExp$matchResult | null;
   390	    while ((match = regex.exec(result)) !== null) {
   391	      if (match == null) continue;
   392	      const ref = match[1];
   393	      if (visited.has(ref)) {
   394	        throw new Error(`circular reference detected for constant ${ref}`);
   395	      }
   396	      const refKey = `var(${ref})`;
   397	      const refValue = constsMap.get(refKey);
   398	      if (refValue == null) continue;
   399	      visited.add(ref);
   400	      const replacement = resolveConstant(refValue, visited);
   401	      result = result.replace(match[0], replacement.toString());
   402	      visited.delete(ref);
   403	      regex.lastIndex = 0;
   404	    }
   405	    return result;
   406	  }
   407	
   408	  for (const [key, value] of constsMap.entries()) {
   409	    constsMap.set(key, resolveConstant(value));
   410	  }
   411	
   412	  const sortedRules = nonConstantRules.sort(
   413	    (
   414	      [, { ltr: rule1 }, firstPriority]: [string, any, number],
   415	      [, { ltr: rule2 }, secondPriority]: [string, any, number],
   416	    ) => {
   417	      const priorityComparison = firstPriority - secondPriority;
   418	      if (priorityComparison !== 0) return priorityComparison;
   419	      if (rule1.startsWith('@') && !rule2.startsWith('@')) {
   420	        const query1 = rule1.slice(0, rule1.indexOf('{'));
   421	        const query2 = rule2.slice(0, rule2.indexOf('{'));
   422	        if (query1 !== query2) {
   423	          return query1.localeCompare(query2);
   424	        }
   425	      }
   426	      const property1 = rule1.slice(rule1.lastIndexOf('{'));
   427	      const property2 = rule2.slice(rule2.lastIndexOf('{'));
   428	      return property1.localeCompare(property2);
   429	    },
   430	  );
   431

Now I understand the flow better. Let me trace through what happens:

1. `breakpoints` is defined via `stylex.defineConsts({ small: '@media (max-width: 600px)', ... })`
2. In `stylex.create`, when we use `[breakpoints.small]` as a computed key in a dynamic style function, the constant gets resolved.

Looking at `evaluate-path.js`, when evaluating an import from a `.stylex.js` file, the function `evaluateImportedFile` evaluates the export. But for `defineConsts` files, the import path resolution in `state-manager.js` returns `['themeNameRef', ...]` when the file has `.stylex` extension.

So the constant value gets resolved via `evaluateThemeRef` which returns a Proxy that generates CSS variable references like `var(--x1r2wpmh)` for each key access.

So `breakpoints.small` resolves to `var(--x1r2wpmh)` (a CSS variable reference).

Now in `evaluatePartialObjectRecursively` (parse-stylex-create-arg.js), when processing the dynamic function, the computed key `[breakpoints.small]` evaluates to `var(--x1r2wpmh)`.

Then the resulting object after evaluation has something like:
```js
{
  transition: {
    'var(--x1r2wpmh)': 'none',
    default: 'transform ${animationDuration}ms ease-in-out'
  }
}
```

This gets passed to `stylexCreate` (stylex-create.js shared), which calls `validateNamespace`. But wait, `validateNamespace` calls `validateConditionalStyles` when it encounters a plain object value for a property key that is NOT a pseudo/at-rule.

The key question is: what does the final evaluated object look like after the `evaluateStyleXCreateArg` returns?

Let me look at `parse-stylex-create-arg.js` more carefully at lines 152-155:

```javascript
if (key.startsWith('var(') && key.endsWith(')')) {
  key = key.slice(4, -1);
}
```

So when the key is `var(--x1r2wpmh)`, it slices off `var(` and `)` to get `--x1r2wpmh`. 

Now, looking at `flatten-raw-style-obj.js` line 47-49:
```javascript
const key: string = _key.match(/var\(--[a-z0-9]+\)/)
  ? _key.slice(4, -1)
  : _key;
```

There's similar handling in `flattenRawStyleObject` as well.

But in `validateConditionalStyles`, the check is:
```javascript
if (
  !(
    key.startsWith('@') ||
    key.startsWith(':') ||
    // This is a placeholder for `defineConsts` values that are later inlined
    key.startsWith('var(--') ||
    key === 'default'
  )
) {
  throw new Error(messages.INVALID_PSEUDO_OR_AT_RULE);
}
```

So the key must start with `@`, `:`, `var(--`, or be `'default'`.

The issue is: When the key from the evaluation is like `var(--x1r2wpmh)`, that should pass the check because `key.startsWith('var(--')` is true.

But wait, looking at `parse-stylex-create-arg.js` lines 152-155 again:
```javascript
if (key.startsWith('var(') && key.endsWith(')')) {
  key = key.slice(4, -1);
}
```

This transforms `var(--x1r2wpmh)` into `--x1r2wpmh`. Now `--x1r2wpmh` does NOT start with `var(--`, `@`, `:`, and is not `'default'`. So it fails the validation!

But wait, there's also the `flattenRawStyleObject` function that handles this at lines 47-49:
```javascript
const key: string = _key.match(/var\(--[a-z0-9]+\)/)
  ? _key.slice(4, -1)
  : _key;
```

This also strips `var(` and `)` from the key. But this happens AFTER validation (since validation is called first at line 57 of stylex-create.js).

Let me check the order of operations. In `stylex-create.js`:

1. `validateNamespace(namespace)` is called at line 57
2. `flattenRawStyleObject` is called at line 64

So validation happens BEFORE the `var(--...)` keys are stripped. So the keys should still be `var(--x1r2wpmh)` at validation time.

But wait, the `evaluatePartialObjectRecursively` already strips the `var(` and `)` prefix/suffix at lines 152-155. So by the time the object reaches `validateNamespace`, the keys have already been transformed from `var(--x1r2wpmh)` to `--x1r2wpmh`.

Let me verify this by adding some debug logging. But first, let me look at what happens for a non-dynamic (static) case that works, like the test `'adds media query placeholder from constants.stylex'`:

```js
stylex.create({
  root: {
    color: {
      default: 'red',
      [breakpoints.small]: 'blue',
    },
  },
```

In this static case, `breakpoints.small` evaluates to `var(--x1r2wpmh)`. This key gets processed in `evaluatePartialObjectRecursively` (since there's no dynamic function). Actually, wait - there's no dynamic function here, so it goes through the regular `evaluate` path. Let me check...

Looking at `evaluateStyleXCreateArg`:
- For static cases (no arrow functions), it goes to line 71-77:
```javascript
if (!valPath.isArrowFunctionExpression()) {
  const val = evaluate(valPath, traversalState, functions);
  if (!val.confident) {
    return val;
  }
  value[key] = val.value;
  continue;
}
```

So static values are evaluated through the `evaluate` function from `evaluate-path.js`. That function evaluates the object and returns the actual JS value. When it encounters `[breakpoints.small]` as a computed key, it resolves `breakpoints.small` to `var(--x1r2wpmh)` and uses that as the key.

Now, in the dynamic case (with arrow functions), the flow goes through `evaluatePartialObjectRecursively` which at line 152-155 strips the `var(` prefix. But in the static case, the evaluation does NOT strip it - it keeps the full `var(--x1r2wpmh)` as the key.

So the difference is:

    20	 *
    21	 * @param {string} str ASCII only
    22	 * @param {number} seed Positive integer only
    23	 * @return {number} 32-bit positive integer hash
    24	 */
    25	function murmurhash2_32_gc(str: string, seed?: number = 0) {
    26	  let l = str.length,
    27	    h = seed ^ l,
    28	    i = 0,
    29	    k;
    30	
    31	  while (l >= 4) {
    32	    k =
    33	      (str.charCodeAt(i) & 0xff) |
    34	      ((str.charCodeAt(++i) & 0xff) << 8) |
    35	      ((str.charCodeAt(++i) & 0xff) << 16) |
    36	      ((str.charCodeAt(++i) & 0xff) << 24);
    37	
    38	    k =
    39	      (k & 0xffff) * 0x5bd1e995 + ((((k >>> 16) * 0x5bd1e995) & 0xffff) << 16);
    40	    k ^= k >>> 24;
    41	    k =
    42	      (k & 0xffff) * 0x5bd1e995 + ((((k >>> 16) * 0x5bd1e995) & 0xffff) << 16);
    43	
    44	    h =
    45	      ((h & 0xffff) * 0x5bd1e995 +
    46	        ((((h >>> 16) * 0x5bd1e995) & 0xffff) << 16)) ^
    47	      k;
    48	
    49	    l -= 4;
    50	    ++i;
    51	  }
    52	
    53	  switch (l) {
    54	    case 3:
    55	      h ^= (str.charCodeAt(i + 2) & 0xff) << 16;
    56	    case 2:
    57	      h ^= (str.charCodeAt(i + 1) & 0xff) << 8;
    58	    case 1:
    59	      h ^= str.charCodeAt(i) & 0xff;
    60	      h =
    61	        (h & 0xffff) * 0x5bd1e995 +
    62	        ((((h >>> 16) * 0x5bd1e995) & 0xffff) << 16);
    63	  }
    64	
    65	  h ^= h >>> 13;
    66	  h = (h & 0xffff) * 0x5bd1e995 + ((((h >>> 16) * 0x5bd1e995) & 0xffff) << 16);
    67	  h ^= h >>> 15;
    68	
    69	  return h >>> 0;
    70	}

    76	const base62Chars =
    77	  '0123456789ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz';
    78	function toBase62(num: number) {
    79	  let result = '';
    80	  let _num = num;
    81	  while (_num > 0) {
    82	    const remainder = _num % 62;
    83	    result = base62Chars[remainder] + result;
    84	    _num = Math.floor(_num / 62);
    85	  }
    86	  return result;
    87	}

The hash produces base-36 (for `hash`) or base-62 (for `createShortHash`) strings, which can contain uppercase letters. So the regex `/var\(--[a-z0-9]+\)/` would NOT match if the hash contains uppercase letters. But looking at the test output, the hashes seem to be lowercase only (like `x1r2wpmh`). The `toString(36)` produces lowercase alphanumeric. So the regex should be fine.

But wait, there's another issue: the regex only matches `[a-z0-9]+` (one or more lowercase alphanumeric). What if the CSS variable name contains hyphens? Like `--x-...` - the hash itself doesn't contain hyphens, but the `--x-` prefix does. The regex `var\(--[a-z0-9]+\)` would match `var(--x1r2wpmh)` because after `--`, the `x1r2wpmh` is alphanumeric. But if the variable name has other characters (like from debug mode), it might not match.

Anyway, this is a side issue. Let me focus on the fix.

Here's another place where `var(` is stripped from the key. This is in `flatMapExpandedShorthands` which is called from `flattenRawStyleObject`. This stripping happens after validation, so it's fine.

Now let me also check the `flattenRawStyleObject` line 47-49 again. It uses a regex:
```javascript
const key: string = _key.match(/var\(--[a-z0-9]+\)/)
  ? _key.slice(4, -1)
  : _key;
```

This regex is more specific - it only matches `var(--...)` with alphanumeric chars. The stripping in `flatMapExpandedShorthands` uses `startsWith('var(') && endsWith(')')` which is more general.

But the key point is that both of these happen AFTER validation. So the validation should see `var(--...)` format keys.

My fix removes the premature stripping in `evaluatePartialObjectRecursively`, which should align it with the static path.

     2	 * Copyright (c) Meta Platforms, Inc. and affiliates.
     3	 *

     6	 *

     8	 */
     9	
    10	const isVar = (arg: string) =>
    11	  typeof arg === 'string' && arg.match(/^var\(--[a-zA-Z0-9-_]+\)$/);
    12	
    13	export default function stylexFirstThatWorks(
    14	  ...args: $ReadOnlyArray<string>
    15	): $ReadOnlyArray<string> | string {
    16	  const firstVar = args.findIndex(isVar);
    17	
    18	  if (firstVar === -1) {
    19	    return [...args].reverse();
    20	  }
    21	  const priorities = args.slice(0, firstVar).reverse();
    22	  const rest = args.slice(firstVar);
    23	  const firstNonVar = rest.findIndex((arg) => !isVar(arg));
    24	  const varParts = rest
    25	    .slice(0, firstNonVar === -1 ? rest.length : firstNonVar + 1)
    26	    .reverse();
    27	
    28	  const vars = varParts.map((arg) => (isVar(arg) ? arg.slice(4, -1) : arg));
    29	
    30	  const returnValue = [
    31	    vars.reduce<string>(
    32	      (soFar, varName) =>
    33	        soFar
    34	          ? `var(${varName}, ${String(soFar)})`
    35	          : varName.startsWith('--')
    36	            ? `var(${varName})`
    37	            : varName,
    38	      '',
    39	    ),
    40	    ...priorities,
    41	  ];
    42	  if (returnValue.length === 1) {
    43	    return returnValue[0];
    44	  }
    45	  return returnValue;
    46	}

So the result is `'var(--x1itgfi6, transparent)'`.

This is a string value for the `color` property. So the object after evaluation should be:
```js
{
  foo: {
    color: 'var(--x1itgfi6, transparent)'
  }
}
```

This should pass validation without issues. The key `color` is not a pseudo/at-rule, but it's at the property level, not conditional level. Let me trace through validation:

1. `validateNamespace` is called with the namespace object
2. The namespace is `{ nodeEnd: { foo: { color: '...' } } }`... wait, no.

Actually, the evaluated result from `evaluateStyleXCreateArg` is:
```js
{
  nodeEnd: [params, inlineStyles]  // This is stored in fns
}
```

And the value is:
```js
{
  foo: {
    color: 'var(--x1itgfi6, transparent)'
  }
}
```

Then `stylexCreate` receives this as the `plainObject`. `validateNamespace` is called on this object.

For `nodeEnd`, the value is `{ foo: { color: '...' } }`. This is a plain object, not starting with `@` or `:`, so `validateConditionalStyles` is called.

In `validateConditionalStyles`, the keys are iterated:
- Key `'foo'` - does it start with `@`, `:`, `var(--`, or is it `'default'`? No! So it throws!

Ah, that's the issue! `'foo'` is a property name, not a conditional. But `validateNamespace` calls `validateConditionalStyles` for any object value that doesn't have `@` or `:` prefix. But `foo` is supposed to be a nested namespace key, not a conditional!

Wait, let me re-read `validateNamespace`:

```javascript
if (isPlainObject(val)) {
  if (key.startsWith('@') || key.startsWith(':')) {
    if (conditions.includes(key)) {
      throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);
    }
    validateNamespace(val, [...conditions, key]);
  } else {
    validateConditionalStyles(val as $FlowFixMe);
  }
  continue;
}
```

So if the key does NOT start with `@` or `:`, it treats the value as `ConditionalStyles` and validates it. But `foo` is a style property key (like `color`, `backgroundColor`), not a conditional. So `validateConditionalStyles` would check if all keys in the object start with `@`, `:`, `var(--`, or are `'default'`. But the keys of `{ color: '...' }` are like `'color'`, which is none of those!

Wait, but the original test case (static) has:
```js
stylex.create({
  root: {
    color: { default: 'red', [breakpoints.small]: 'blue' }
  }
});
```

Here, `root`'s value is `{ color: { default: 'red', [breakpoints.small]: 'blue' } }`. The key `root` doesn't start with `@` or `:`, so `validateConditionalStyles` is called on `{ color: { default: 'red', [breakpoints.small]: 'blue' } }`. The keys are `'color'`. Does `'color'` pass? No, it doesn't start with `@`, `:`, `var(--`, and is not `'default'`.

But this test passes! How?

Let me look at `validateConditionalStyles` again more carefully:

```javascript
function validateConditionalStyles(
  val: ConditionalStyles,
  conditions: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
): void {
  for (const key in val) {
    const v = val[key];
    if (
      !(
        key.startsWith('@') ||
        key.startsWith(':') ||
        key.startsWith('var(--') ||
        key === 'default'
      )
    ) {
      throw new Error(messages.INVALID_PSEUDO_OR_AT_RULE);
    }
    if (conditions.includes(key)) {
      throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);
    }
    if (v === null || typeof v === 'string' || typeof v === 'number') {
      continue;
    }
    if (Array.isArray(v)) {
      // ...
    }
    if (isPlainObject(v)) {
      validateConditionalStyles(v, [...conditions, key]);
      continue;
    }
    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
  }
}
```
